Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageErickson Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.ericksonseniorliving.com/contact
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score854
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 854, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 180. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 200. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue targetSize

WCAG: 2.5.5

Score: 92

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 152, score 90 (Actionable element is smaller than the minimum required size)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 42

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 11 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 36 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 36

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 34 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue errorReferenceBad

WCAG: 3.3.1

Score: 31

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R41, score 29 (Error message describes no invalid form field value)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 30

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 28 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue iframeTitleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 228, score 4 (iframe has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.2_4_1.H64.1, score 16 (iframe element has no non-empty title attribute)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 18 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue titleBad

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 14

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test titledEl, score 12 (title attribute belongs to an inappropriate element)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 10

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 8 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue svgImageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 10

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 123, score 8 (svg element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)

Issue linkTextsSame

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 10

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R9, score 1 (Links with identical accessible names have different purposes)
  • Package tenon, test 98, score 8 (Links have the same text but different destinations)

Issue roleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test role, score 6 (Nonexistent or implicit-overriding role)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test link-name, score 3 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 4 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.Empty, score 1 (a element has an id attribute but no href attribute or text)

Score: 7

  • Package tenon, test 155, score 1 (Headings are not structured in a hierarchical manner)

Issue repeatedContentRisk

WCAG: 2.4.1

Score: 6

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R73, score 1 (Block of repeated content is not collapsible)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R74, score 1 (Document has no instrument to move focus to non-repeated content)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-WCAG-T23, score 1 (No link at the top of the page that goes directly to the main content area)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-BP17, score 1 (No link at the beginning of a block of repeated content goes to the end of the block)
